commi_antagonize_KMX = {
	enable = {
		has_government = communism
		KMX = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
		KMX = { exists = yes }
	}
	abort = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
			KMX = { exists = no }
			KMX = { has_government = communism }
		}
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = antagonize
		id = "KMX" 
		value = 200
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = alliance
		id = "KMX" 
		value = -5000
	}
}

no_boost_balkanization_bul = {
	enable = {
		ROOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				NOT = {
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				original_tag = TUR
				original_tag = TRK
			}
		}
		BUL = {
			has_completed_focus = BUL_balkan_alliance
			is_faction_leader = yes
		}
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	
	ai_strategy = {
		type = alliance
		id = "BUL" 
		value = -500
	}
}

## Игровые правила ##

#AI_FACTION_LOWER

rule_option_ai_faction_lower_GER = { reversed = yes enable = { has_game_rule = { rule = ai_faction_status option = AI_FACTION_LOWER } NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } } abort_when_not_enabled = yes ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "GER" value = -75 } }
rule_option_ai_faction_lower_ENG = { reversed = yes enable = { has_game_rule = { rule = ai_faction_status option = AI_FACTION_LOWER } NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG } } abort_when_not_enabled = yes ai_strategy = { type = alliance id = "ENG" value = -75 } }
